\ttx.RLock()\n189: \tdefer tx.RUnlock()\n190: \ts.mu.RUnlock()\n191: \thash, err = unsafeHashByRev(tx, compactRev, rev, keep)\n192: \thashRevSec.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n193: \treturn rc.retention\n82: \t\t\tif rev <= 0 || rev == prev {\n83: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n84: \t\t\t}\n85: \n86: \t\t\tnow := time.Now()\n87: \t\t\trc.lg.Info(\n88: \t\t\t\t\"starting auto revision compaction\",\n89: \t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n90: \t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision-compaction-retention\", rc.retention),\n91: \t\t\t)\n92: \t\t\t_, err := rc.c.Compact(rc.ctx, &pb.CompactionRequest{Revision: rev})\n93: \t\t\tif err == nil || errors.Is(err, mvcc.ErrCompacted) {\n94: \t\t\t\tprev = rev\n95: \t\t\t\trc.lg.Info(\n96: \t\t\t\t\t\"completed auto revision compaction\",\n97: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n98: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision-compaction-retention\", rc.retention),\n99: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"took\", time.Since(now)),\n100: \t\t\t\t)\n101: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/etcd-io/etcd@ebf40472ef8515dfa9202eb813b2e9c5dbd035a1/-/blob/server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go%3FL1-100"}}}

Overview\\nThe etcd MVCC compaction system consists of three main components: (1) compaction scheduling (periodic vs revision-based), (2) compaction of revision indices and data, and (3) notification of watch streams that span a compacted revision with slow watch detection.\\n\\n## Compaction Schedule (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/)\\n\\n### Compactor Interface (compactor.go)\\nDefines the `Compactor` interface with `Run()` and `Stop()` methods. Two implementations exist:\\n\\n### Periodic Compaction (periodic.go)\\nImplements time-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Records revisions at 1/10th of the retention period\\n- **Interval**: Compaction happens every hour for periods ≥1 hour, or every retention period for periods <1 hour\\n- **Algorithm**: Maintains a sliding window of revisions, compacting oldest revision when retention period expires\\n- **Key struct**: `Periodic` with fields `period`, `revs` (revision history), `clock`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable)\\n\\n### Revision-Based Compaction (revision.go)\\nImplements revision count-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Runs every 5 minutes\\n- **Calculation**: Compacts at `current_revision - retention`\\n- **Key struct**: `Revision` with fields `retention`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable), `clock`\\n\\n## Compaction Process (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Core Compaction Flow\\n\\n1. **Initiation** (kvstore.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev)`: Public method that locks the store and calls `compactLockfree()`\\n   - `compactLockfree(rev)`: Acquires write lock, calls `updateCompactRev()`, then `compact()`\\n   - `updateCompactRev(rev)`: Updates `compactMainRev`, persists via `SetScheduledCompact()` to backend\\n   - `checkPrevCompactionCompleted()`: Ensures previous compaction finished before starting new one\\n\\n2. **Index Compaction** (index.go, key_index.go)\\n   - `treeIndex.Compact(rev)`: Iterates all keys, calls `keyIndex.compact()` for each\\n   - `keyIndex.compact(lg, atRev, available)`: Removes versions ≤ atRev, keeps largest one; removes empty generations\\n   - `doCompact(atRev, available)`: Walks through generations to find which revisions to keep\\n   - `treeIndex.Keep(rev)`: Identifies revisions to preserve during compaction\\n   - **Result**: `keep` map contains all revisions that must be preserved\\n\\n3. **Data Compaction** (kvstore_compaction.go)\\n   - `scheduleCompaction(compactMainRev, prevCompactRev)`: Main compaction worker\\n   - **Process**:\\n     1. Compacts kvindex via `Keep()` to get revisions to preserve\\n     2. Iterates through backend key-value store in batches\\n     3. Deletes keys for revisions not in `keep` map\\n     4. Computes hash incrementally via `newKVHasher`\\n     5. Commits batches with sleep interval between them\\n     6. Sets `FinishedCompact` metadata when done\\n   - **Metrics**: Tracks `indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`, `dbCompactionLast`\\n\\n4. **Scheduled Compaction Tracking** (store.go)\\n   - `SetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Writes scheduled revision to backend meta bucket\\n   - `UnsafeSetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Unsafe version for batch transactions\\n   - `UnsafeReadScheduledCompact(tx)`: Reads scheduled compaction revision from backend\\n\\n## Watch Stream Notification (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Watch Stream Architecture\\n\\n1. **Watcher Types** (watchable_store.go, watcher.go, watcher_group.go)\\n   - **Synced watchers**: Keep up with current store revisions, in `synced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Unsynced watchers** (slow watchers): Behind current revision, in `unsynced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Victim watchers**: Blocked on send channel, stored separately for retry\\n\\n2. **Watch Stream Registration** (watchable_store.go:127)\\n   - `watch(key, end, startRev, id, ch, fcs)` creates watcher\\n   - If `startRev > currentRev` or `startRev == 0`: goes to `synced` group\\n   - Otherwise: goes to `unsynced` group, increments `slowWatcherGauge`\\n\\n### Compaction Notification Flow\\n\\n1. **Syncing Unsynced Watchers** (watchable_store.go:346)\\n   - `syncWatchersLoop()`: Runs every 100ms (watchResyncPeriod)\\n   - `syncWatchers(evs)`: Batches up to 512 unsynced watchers\\n   - For each batch:\\n     1. Calls `unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)`\\n     2. `choose()` detects and removes watchers with `minRev < compactionRev`\\n     3. Sends `WatchResponse{CompactRevision: compactionRev}` to compacted watchers\\n     4. Sets `w.compacted = true` and removes from group\\n\\n2. **Compaction Detection** (watcher_group.go:237-266)\\n   - `chooseAll(curRev, compactRev)`: Iterates all watchers in group\\n   - For each watcher: if `w.minRev < compactRev`:\\n     - Sends `WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, CompactRevision: compactRev}` to channel\\n     - Sets `w.compacted = true` \\n     - Removes watcher from group\\n   - Handles channel blocking with `default` case to retry later\\n\\n3. **Watch Response During Transactions** (watchable_store_txn.go)\\n   - `watchableStoreTxnWrite.End()` calls `notify(rev, evs)` under lock\\n   - Sends normal events only to synced watchers\\n   - Blocked watchers become victims and are retried by `syncVictimsLoop()`\\n\\n### Watch Progress Notification\\n\\n1. **Progress Tracking** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - `progressIfSync(watchers, responseWatchID)`: Sends progress notifications when all watchers synced\\n   - `progress(w)`: Requests progress for specific watcher\\n   - `progressAll(watchers)`: Broadcasts progress to all watchers\\n   - Sent as empty WatchResponse with only revision set\\n\\n2. **Progress Interval** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - Configurable via `WatchProgressNotifyInterval` flag\\n   - Minimum 100ms, default 10 minutes\\n   - Allows clients to track server progress even without events\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n1. **Metrics** (metrics.go)\\n   - `slowWatcherGauge`: Prometheus gauge tracking number of unsynced (slow) watchers\\n   - Incremented when watcher added to `unsynced` group (line 148 in watchable_store.go)\\n   - Decremented when moved to `synced` or when victim processing completes\\n   - Set from victim batch size in `syncWatchers()` (line 411)\\n\\n2. **Slow Watcher Identification**\\n   - Any watcher with `minRev < currentRev` at creation time\\n   - Any watcher that becomes blocked on send channel (becomes victim)\\n   - Separate tracking in `unsynced` watcherGroup distinct from `synced`\\n   - `maxWatchersPerSync = 512`: Limits batch size for fairness\\n\\n3. **Victim Processing** (watchable_store.go:257-339)\\n   - `syncVictimsLoop()`: Continuously retries blocked watchers\\n   - `moveVictims()`: Attempts to send queued responses again\\n   - Victims in separate `victims` list (watcherBatch)\\n   - Retried every 10ms if any victims exist\\n\\n## Related Components\\n\\n1. **Hash Computation** (hash.go)\\n   - `KeyValueHash`: Contains hash, revision, and compactRevision fields\\n   - Incremental hash calculation during compaction via `newKVHasher`\\n   - Allows corruption detection across cluster members\\n\\n2. **API** (server/etcdserver/v3_server.go)\\n   - `Compact(ctx, request)`: RPC handler for explicit compaction requests\\n   - Calls store `Compact()` method with requested revision\\n   - Supports `Physical` flag for synchronous completion\\n\\n3. **KV Interface** (kv.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev) (<-chan struct{}, error)`: Asynchronous compaction with channel for completion signal\\n   - Part of MVCC KV store interface\\n\\n## Key Data Structures\\n\\n- **watchableStore**: Contains `synced` and `unsynced` watcherGroups, `victims` list\\n- **watcherGroup**: Organizes watchers by key ranges using interval trees, enables efficient notification\\n- **watcher**: Individual watch with `minRev`, `startRev`, channel, filter functions, and `compacted` flag\\n- **Revision**: Struct with Main and Sub fields for comparing versions\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nEtcd's MVCC compaction is a sophisticated system that:\\n1. Schedules compaction either periodically (time-based) or by revision count\\n2. Performs index and data compaction in batches with sleep intervals to avoid blocking\\n3. Notifies watch streams of compaction via separate handling in watcher groups\\n4. Detects and tracks slow (unsynced) watchers separately from synced ones\\n5. Implements victim/retry pattern for blocked watchers\\n6. Provides progress notifications to allow clients to stay informed of server progress\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2829,"cache_read_input_tokens":91948,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2829},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b1426820-a89f-4afa-81bc-48560f660ab9","uuid":"7ec0334d-ec1e-40fd-a99b-4f321ea10cbe"}

Overview\\nThe etcd MVCC compaction system consists of three main components: (1) compaction scheduling (periodic vs revision-based), (2) compaction of revision indices and data, and (3) notification of watch streams that span a compacted revision with slow watch detection.\\n\\n## Compaction Schedule (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/)\\n\\n### Compactor Interface (compactor.go)\\nDefines the `Compactor` interface with `Run()` and `Stop()` methods. Two implementations exist:\\n\\n### Periodic Compaction (periodic.go)\\nImplements time-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Records revisions at 1/10th of the retention period\\n- **Interval**: Compaction happens every hour for periods ≥1 hour, or every retention period for periods <1 hour\\n- **Algorithm**: Maintains a sliding window of revisions, compacting oldest revision when retention period expires\\n- **Key struct**: `Periodic` with fields `period`, `revs` (revision history), `clock`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable)\\n\\n### Revision-Based Compaction (revision.go)\\nImplements revision count-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Runs every 5 minutes\\n- **Calculation**: Compacts at `current_revision - retention`\\n- **Key struct**: `Revision` with fields `retention`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable), `clock`\\n\\n## Compaction Process (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Core Compaction Flow\\n\\n1. **Initiation** (kvstore.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev)`: Public method that locks the store and calls `compactLockfree()`\\n   - `compactLockfree(rev)`: Acquires write lock, calls `updateCompactRev()`, then `compact()`\\n   - `updateCompactRev(rev)`: Updates `compactMainRev`, persists via `SetScheduledCompact()` to backend\\n   - `checkPrevCompactionCompleted()`: Ensures previous compaction finished before starting new one\\n\\n2. **Index Compaction** (index.go, key_index.go)\\n   - `treeIndex.Compact(rev)`: Iterates all keys, calls `keyIndex.compact()` for each\\n   - `keyIndex.compact(lg, atRev, available)`: Removes versions ≤ atRev, keeps largest one; removes empty generations\\n   - `doCompact(atRev, available)`: Walks through generations to find which revisions to keep\\n   - `treeIndex.Keep(rev)`: Identifies revisions to preserve during compaction\\n   - **Result**: `keep` map contains all revisions that must be preserved\\n\\n3. **Data Compaction** (kvstore_compaction.go)\\n   - `scheduleCompaction(compactMainRev, prevCompactRev)`: Main compaction worker\\n   - **Process**:\\n     1. Compacts kvindex via `Keep()` to get revisions to preserve\\n     2. Iterates through backend key-value store in batches\\n     3. Deletes keys for revisions not in `keep` map\\n     4. Computes hash incrementally via `newKVHasher`\\n     5. Commits batches with sleep interval between them\\n     6. Sets `FinishedCompact` metadata when done\\n   - **Metrics**: Tracks `indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`, `dbCompactionLast`\\n\\n4. **Scheduled Compaction Tracking** (store.go)\\n   - `SetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Writes scheduled revision to backend meta bucket\\n   - `UnsafeSetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Unsafe version for batch transactions\\n   - `UnsafeReadScheduledCompact(tx)`: Reads scheduled compaction revision from backend\\n\\n## Watch Stream Notification (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Watch Stream Architecture\\n\\n1. **Watcher Types** (watchable_store.go, watcher.go, watcher_group.go)\\n   - **Synced watchers**: Keep up with current store revisions, in `synced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Unsynced watchers** (slow watchers): Behind current revision, in `unsynced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Victim watchers**: Blocked on send channel, stored separately for retry\\n\\n2. **Watch Stream Registration** (watchable_store.go:127)\\n   - `watch(key, end, startRev, id, ch, fcs)` creates watcher\\n   - If `startRev > currentRev` or `startRev == 0`: goes to `synced` group\\n   - Otherwise: goes to `unsynced` group, increments `slowWatcherGauge`\\n\\n### Compaction Notification Flow\\n\\n1. **Syncing Unsynced Watchers** (watchable_store.go:346)\\n   - `syncWatchersLoop()`: Runs every 100ms (watchResyncPeriod)\\n   - `syncWatchers(evs)`: Batches up to 512 unsynced watchers\\n   - For each batch:\\n     1. Calls `unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)`\\n     2. `choose()` detects and removes watchers with `minRev < compactionRev`\\n     3. Sends `WatchResponse{CompactRevision: compactionRev}` to compacted watchers\\n     4. Sets `w.compacted = true` and removes from group\\n\\n2. **Compaction Detection** (watcher_group.go:237-266)\\n   - `chooseAll(curRev, compactRev)`: Iterates all watchers in group\\n   - For each watcher: if `w.minRev < compactRev`:\\n     - Sends `WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, CompactRevision: compactRev}` to channel\\n     - Sets `w.compacted = true` \\n     - Removes watcher from group\\n   - Handles channel blocking with `default` case to retry later\\n\\n3. **Watch Response During Transactions** (watchable_store_txn.go)\\n   - `watchableStoreTxnWrite.End()` calls `notify(rev, evs)` under lock\\n   - Sends normal events only to synced watchers\\n   - Blocked watchers become victims and are retried by `syncVictimsLoop()`\\n\\n### Watch Progress Notification\\n\\n1. **Progress Tracking** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - `progressIfSync(watchers, responseWatchID)`: Sends progress notifications when all watchers synced\\n   - `progress(w)`: Requests progress for specific watcher\\n   - `progressAll(watchers)`: Broadcasts progress to all watchers\\n   - Sent as empty WatchResponse with only revision set\\n\\n2. **Progress Interval** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - Configurable via `WatchProgressNotifyInterval` flag\\n   - Minimum 100ms, default 10 minutes\\n   - Allows clients to track server progress even without events\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n1. **Metrics** (metrics.go)\\n   - `slowWatcherGauge`: Prometheus gauge tracking number of unsynced (slow) watchers\\n   - Incremented when watcher added to `unsynced` group (line 148 in watchable_store.go)\\n   - Decremented when moved to `synced` or when victim processing completes\\n   - Set from victim batch size in `syncWatchers()` (line 411)\\n\\n2. **Slow Watcher Identification**\\n   - Any watcher with `minRev < currentRev` at creation time\\n   - Any watcher that becomes blocked on send channel (becomes victim)\\n   - Separate tracking in `unsynced` watcherGroup distinct from `synced`\\n   - `maxWatchersPerSync = 512`: Limits batch size for fairness\\n\\n3. **Victim Processing** (watchable_store.go:257-339)\\n   - `syncVictimsLoop()`: Continuously retries blocked watchers\\n   - `moveVictims()`: Attempts to send queued responses again\\n   - Victims in separate `victims` list (watcherBatch)\\n   - Retried every 10ms if any victims exist\\n\\n## Related Components\\n\\n1. **Hash Computation** (hash.go)\\n   - `KeyValueHash`: Contains hash, revision, and compactRevision fields\\n   - Incremental hash calculation during compaction via `newKVHasher`\\n   - Allows corruption detection across cluster members\\n\\n2. **API** (server/etcdserver/v3_server.go)\\n   - `Compact(ctx, request)`: RPC handler for explicit compaction requests\\n   - Calls store `Compact()` method with requested revision\\n   - Supports `Physical` flag for synchronous completion\\n\\n3. **KV Interface** (kv.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev) (<-chan struct{}, error)`: Asynchronous compaction with channel for completion signal\\n   - Part of MVCC KV store interface\\n\\n## Key Data Structures\\n\\n- **watchableStore**: Contains `synced` and `unsynced` watcherGroups, `victims` list\\n- **watcherGroup**: Organizes watchers by key ranges using interval trees, enables efficient notification\\n- **watcher**: Individual watch with `minRev`, `startRev`, channel, filter functions, and `compacted` flag\\n- **Revision**: Struct with Main and Sub fields for comparing versions\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nEtcd's MVCC compaction is a sophisticated system that:\\n1. Schedules compaction either periodically (time-based) or by revision count\\n2. Performs index and data compaction in batches with sleep intervals to avoid blocking\\n3. Notifies watch streams of compaction via separate handling in watcher groups\\n4. Detects and tracks slow (unsynced) watchers separately from synced ones\\n5. Implements victim/retry pattern for blocked watchers\\n6. Provides progress notifications to allow clients to stay informed of server progress\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
